BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Look for video information in script tags (YouTube embeds data in JSON)\n            script_tags = len(\'var ytInitialData = \')\n                    end_idx = script_content.find(\'};\', start_idx) + 1\n                    \n                    if start_idx > 0 and end_idx > start_idx:\n                        try:\n                            json_str = script_content[start_idx:end_idx]\n                            data = json.loads(json_str)\n                            \n                            # Navigate YouTube\'s data structure to find videos\n                            contents = data.get(\'contents\', {}).get(\'twoColumnSearchResultsRenderer\', {}).get(\'primaryContents\', {}).get(\'sectionListRenderer\', {}).get(\'contents\', [])\n                            \n                            for section in contents:\n                                items = section.get(\'itemSectionRenderer\', {}).get(\'contents\', [])\n                                \n                                for item in items:\n                                    if \'videoRenderer\' in item:\n                                        video = item[\'videoRenderer\']\n                                        \n                                        # Extract video information\n                                        video_info = {\n                                            \'title\': video.get(\'title\', {}).get(\'runs\', [{}])[0].get(\'text\', \'Unknown title\'),\n                                            \'video_id\': video.get(\'videoId\', \'\'),\n                                            \'url\': f"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v={video.get(\'videoId\', \'\')}",\n                                            \'channel\': video.get(\'ownerText\', {}).get(\'runs\', [{}])[0].get(\'text\', \'Unknown channel\'),\n                                            \'duration\': video.get(\'lengthText\', {}).get(\'simpleText\', \'Unknown duration\'),\n                                            \'views\': video.get(\'viewCountText\', {}).get(\'simpleText\', \'Unknown views\'),\n                                            \'description\': video.get(\'descriptionSnippet\', {}).get(\'runs\',  videos_found.append(video_info)\n                                        \n                                        if len(videos_found) >= max_results:\n                                            break\n                                \n                                if len(videos_found) >= max_results:\n                                    break\n                            \n                            break  # Found the data we need\n                            \n                        except json.JSONDecodeError:\n                            continue\n            \n            print(f"Found {len(videos_found)} videos\\n")\n            return videos_found\n            \n        else:\n            print(f"Failed to fetch search results: HTTP {response.status_code}\\n")\n Make API request to SerpAPI\n        response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30)\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            results = response.json()\n            organic_results = results.get("organic_results", [])\n            \n            print(f"  → Found {len(organic_results)} results")\n            \n            # Filter for YouTube videos and analyze relevance\n            youtube_results = []\n            for result in organic_results:\n                link = result.get(\'link\', \'\')\n                title = result.get(\'title\', \'\')\n                snippet = result.get(\'snippet\', \'\')\n                \n                # Focus on YouTube videos\n                if \'youtube.com/watch\' in link:\n                    # Analyze relevance for covers of established songs\n                    relevance_score = 0\n                    title_lower = title.lower()\n                    snippet_lower = snippet.lower()\n                    combined_text = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}"\n                    \n                    # Check for rooster/chicken presence\n                    rooster_terms = [\'rooster\', \'chicken\', \'cock\']\n                    has_rooster = any(term in combined_text for term in rooster_terms)\n                    if has_rooster:\n                        relevance_score += 2\n                    \n                    # Check for hamster presence\n                    hamster_terms = [\'hamster\', \'gerbil\', \'guinea pig\']\n                    has_hamster = any(term in combined_text for term in hamster_terms)\n                    if has_hamster:\n                        relevance_score += 2\n                    \n                    # Check for established song indicators\n                    established_indicators = [\'cover\', \'version\', \'parody\', \'nursery rhyme\', \'classic\', \'traditional\', \'disney\', \'christmas\']\n                    has_established = any(indicator in combined_text for indicator in established_indicators)\n                    if has_established:\n                        relevance_score += 2\n                    \n                    # Check for animation indicators\n                    animation_terms = [\'animated\', \'cartoon\', \'animation\', \'3d\', \'cgi\']\n                    has_animated = any(term in combined_text for term in animation_terms)\n                    if has_animated:\n                        relevance_score += 1\n                    \n                    # Check for singing/music indicators\n                    music_terms = [\'singing\', \'song\', \'music\', \'cover\', \'performance\']\n                    has_music = any(term in combined_text for term in music_terms)\n                    if has_music:\n                        relevance_score += 1\n                    \n                    # Only include results with some relevance\n                    if relevance_score >= 3:\n                        video_data = {\n                            \'query\': query,\n                            \'title\': title,\n                            \'url\': link,\n                            \'snippet\': snippet,\n                            \'relevance_score\': relevance_score,\n                            \'has_rooster\': has_rooster,\n                            \'has_hamster\': has_hamster,\n                            \'has_established_song\': has_established,\n                            \'has_animated\': has_animated,\n                            \'has_music\': has_music\n                        }\n                        youtube_results.append(video_data)\n                        all_relevant_videos.append(video_data)\n            \n            established_song_results[query] = youtube_results\n            \n            if youtube_results:\n                print(f"  → {len(youtube_results)} relevant YouTube videos found")\n                for video in youtube_results[:2]:  # (Score: {video[\'relevance_score\']})")\n            else:\n                print(f"  → No relevant YouTube videos found")\n        \n        else:\n            print(f"  → API request failed: {response.status_code}")\n            established_song_results[query] = []\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"  → Error: {str(e)}")\n        established_song_results[query] = []\n    \n    print()  # Make API request to SerpAPI\n        response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30)\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            results = response.json()\n            organic_results = results.get("organic_results", [])\n            \n            print(f"  → Found {len(organic_results)} results")\n            \n            # Filter and analyze results for relevance\n            relevant_results = []\n            for result in organic_results:\n                link = result.get(\'link\', \'\')\n                title = result.get(\'title\', \'\')\n                snippet = result.get(\'snippet\', \'\')\n                \n                # Analyze relevance for Hampsterdance and Whistle Stop connections\n                relevance_score = 0\n                title_lower = title.lower()\n                snippet_lower = snippet.lower()\n                combined_text = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}"\n                \n                # Check for Hampsterdance references\n                hampster_terms = [\'hampsterdance\', \'hamster dance\', \'dancing hamsters\', \'deedee-deedee-doo\']\n                has_hampsterdance = any(term in combined_text for term in hampster_terms)\n                if has_hampsterdance:\n                    relevance_score += 3\n                \n                # Check for Roger Miller references\n                roger_miller_terms = [\'roger miller\', \'whistle stop\', \'robin hood\']\n                has_roger_miller = any(term in combined_text for term in roger_miller_terms)\n                if has_roger_miller:\n                    relevance_score += 3\n                \n                # Check for Disney connection\n                disney_terms = [\'disney\', \'robin hood\', \'animated movie\']\n                has_disney = any(term in combined_text for term in disney_terms)\n                if has_disney:\n                    relevance_score += 2\n                \n                # Check for rooster/chicken presence\n                rooster_terms = [\'rooster\', \'chicken\', \'cock\']\n                has_rooster = any(term in combined_text for term in rooster_terms)\n                if has_rooster:\n                    relevance_score += 2\n                \n                # Check for animation/viral content\n                viral_terms = [\'viral\', \'animated\', \'internet\', \'meme\', \'phenomenon\']\n                has_viral = any(term in combined_text for term in viral_terms)\n                if has_viral:\n                    relevance_score += 1\n                \n                # Only include results with significant relevance\n                if relevance_score >= 3:\n                    result_data = {\n                        \'query\': query,\n                        \'title\': title,\n                        \'url\': link,\n                        \'snippet\': snippet,\n                        \'relevance_score\': relevance_score,\n                        \'has_hampsterdance\': has_hampsterdance,\n                        \'has_roger_miller\': has_roger_miller,\n                        \'has_disney\': has_disney,\n                        \'has_rooster\': has_rooster,\n                        \'has_viral\': has_viral\n                    }\n                    relevant_results.append(result_data)\n                    all_relevant_videos.append(result_data)\n            \n            hampsterdance_results[query] = relevant_results\n            \n            if relevant_results:\n                print(f"  → {len(relevant_results)} relevant results found")\n                for result in relevant_results[:2]:  # {response.status_code}")\n            hampsterdance_results[query] = []\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"  → Error: {str(e)}")\n        hampsterdance_results[query] = []\n    \n Analyze relevance for Crazy Frog and Axel F connections\n                relevance_score = 0\n                title_lower = title.lower()\n                snippet_lower = snippet.lower()\n                combined_text = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}"\n                \n                #
